\begin{dmath}Pwall = \left(gama - 1\right) \,.\, \left(- \frac{1}{{\rho{_{B0}}}[{0}]} \,.\, \left(\frac{\left({rhou_{0}{_{B0}}}[{0}] \right)^{2}}{2} + \frac{\left({rhou_{1}{_{B0}}}[{0}] \right)^{2}}{2}\right) + {rhoE{_{B0}}}[{0}]\right)\end{dmath}
